Pods from non-apiserver sources are called static pods, and API\\n35: // server is not aware of the existence of static pods. In order to monitor\\n36: // the status of such pods, the kubelet creates a mirror pod for each static\\n37: // pod via the API server.\\n38: //\\n39: // A mirror pod has the same pod full name (name and namespace) as its static\\n40: // counterpart (albeit different metadata such as UID, etc). By leveraging the\\n41: // fact that the kubelet reports the pod status using the pod full name, the\\n42: // status of the mirror pod always reflects the actual status of the static\\n43: // pod. When a static pod gets deleted, the associated orphaned mirror pod\\n44: // will also be removed.\\n45: type Manager interface {\\n46: \\t// GetPodByFullName returns the (non-mirror) pod that matches full name, as well as\\n47: \\t// whether the pod was found.\\n48: \\tGetPodByFullName(podFullName string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n49: \\t// GetPodByName provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches namespace and\\n50: \\t// name, as well as whether the pod was found.\\n51: \\tGetPodByName(namespace, name string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n52: \\t// GetPodByUID provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches pod UID, as well as\\n53: \\t// whether the pod is found.\\n54: \\tGetPodByUID(types.UID) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n55: \\t// GetPodByMirrorPod returns the static pod for the given mirror pod and\\n56: \\t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\\n57: \\tGetPodByMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n58: \\t// GetMirrorPodByPod returns the mirror pod for the given static pod and\\n59: \\t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\\n60: \\tGetMirrorPodByPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n61: \\t// GetPodAndMirrorPod returns the complement for a pod - if a pod was provided\\n62: \\t// and a mirror pod can be found, return it. If a mirror pod is provided and\\n63: \\t// the pod can be found, return it and true for wasMirror.\\n64: \\tGetPodAndMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (pod, mirrorPod *v1.Pod, wasMirror bool)\\n65: \\n66: \\t// GetPods returns the regular pods bound to the kubelet and their spec.\\n67: \\tGetPods() []*v1.Pod\\n68: \\n69: \\t// GetPodsAndMirrorPods returns the set of pods, the set of mirror pods, and\\n70: \\t// the pod fullnames of any orphaned mirror pods.\\n71: \\tGetPodsAndMirrorPods() (allPods []*v1.Pod, allMirrorPods []*v1.Pod, orphanedMirrorPodFullnames []string)\\n72: \\n73: \\t// GetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap return a map of static pod to its corresponding\\n74: \\t// mirror pods. It is possible that there is no mirror pod for a static pod\\n75: \\t// if kubelet is running in standalone mode or is in the process of creating\\n76: \\t// the mirror pod and in that case, the mirror pod is nil.\\n77: \\tGetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap() map[*v1.Pod]*v1.Pod\\n78: \\n79: \\t// SetPods replaces the internal pods with the new pods.\\n80: \\t// It is currently only used for testing.\\n81: \\tSetPods(pods []*v1.Pod)\\n82: \\t// AddPod adds the given pod to the manager.\\n83: \\tAddPod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n84: \\t// UpdatePod updates the given pod in the manager.\\n85: \\tUpdatePod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n86: \\t// RemovePod deletes the given pod from the manager.  For mirror pods,\\n87: \\t// this means deleting the mappings related to mirror pods.  For non-\\n88: \\t// mirror pods, this means deleting from indexes for all non-mirror pods.\\n89: \\tRemovePod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n90: \\n91: \\t// TranslatePodUID returns the actual UID of a pod. If the UID belongs to\\n92: \\t// a mirror pod, returns the UID of its static pod. Otherwise, returns the\\n93: \\t// original UID.\\n94: \\t//\\n95: \\t// All public-facing functions should perform this translation for UIDs\\n96: \\t// because user may provide a mirror pod UID, which is not recognized by\\n97: \\t// internal Kubelet functions.\\n98: \\tTranslatePodUID(uid types.UID) kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID\\n99: \\t// GetUIDTranslations returns the mappings of static pod UIDs to mirror pod\\n100: \\t// UIDs and mirror pod UIDs to static pod UIDs.\\n101: \\tGetUIDTranslations() (podToMirror map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]kubetypes.MirrorPodUID, mirrorToPod map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID)\\n102: }\\n103: \\n104: // basicManager is a functional Manager.\\n105: //\\n106: // All fields in basicManager are read-only and are updated \\t\\\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/metrics\\\"\\n27: \\tkubetypes \\\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/types\\\"\\n28: )\\n29: \\n30: // Manager stores and manages access to pods, maintaining the mappings\\n31: // between static pods and mirror pods.\\n32: //\\n33: // The kubelet discovers pod updates from 3 sources: file, http, and\\n34: // apiserver. Pods from non-apiserver sources are called static pods, and API\\n35: // server is not aware of the existence of static pods. In order to monitor\\n36: // the status of such pods, the kubelet creates a mirror pod for each static\\n37: // pod via the API server.\\n38: //\\n39: // A mirror pod has the same pod full name (name and namespace) as its static\\n40: // counterpart (albeit different metadata such as UID, etc). By leveraging the\\n41: // fact that the kubelet reports the pod status using the pod full name, the\\n42: // status of the mirror pod always reflects the actual status of the static\\n43: // pod. When a static pod gets deleted, the associated orphaned mirror pod\\n44: // will also be removed.\\n45: type Manager interface {\\n46: \\t// GetPodByFullName returns the (non-mirror) pod that matches full name, as well as\\n47: \\t// whether the pod was found.\\n48: \\tGetPodByFullName(podFullName string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n49: \\t// GetPodByName provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches namespace and\\n50: \\t// name, as well as whether the pod was found.\\n51: \\tGetPodByName(namespace, name string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n52: \\t// GetPodByUID provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches pod UID, as well as\\n53: \\t// whether the pod is found.\\n54: \\tGetPodByUID(types.UID) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n55: \\t// GetPodByMirrorPod returns the static pod for the given mirror pod and\\n56: \\t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\\n57: \\tGetPodByMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n58: \\t// GetMirrorPodByPod returns the mirror pod for the given static pod and\\n59: \\t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\\n60: \\tGetMirrorPodByPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n61: \\t// GetPodAndMirrorPod returns the complement for a pod - if a pod was provided\\n62: \\t// and a mirror pod can be found, return it. It is possible that there is no mirror pod for a static pod\\n75: \\t// if kubelet is running in standalone mode or is in the process of creating\\n76: \\t// the mirror pod and in that case, the mirror pod is nil.\\n77: \\tGetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap() map[*v1.Pod]*v1.Pod\\n78: \\n79: \\t// SetPods replaces the internal pods with the new pods.\\n80: \\t// It is currently only used for testing.\\n81: \\tSetPods(pods []*v1.Pod)\\n82: \\t// AddPod adds the given pod to the manager.\\n83: \\tAddPod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n84: \\t// UpdatePod updates the given pod in the manager.\\n85: \\tUpdatePod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n86: \\t// RemovePod deletes the given pod from the manager. \t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types\"\n25: \tkubecontainer \"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/container\"\n26: \t\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/metrics\"\n27: \tkubetypes \"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/types\"\n28: )\n29: \n30: // Manager stores and manages access to pods, maintaining the mappings\n31: // between static pods and mirror pods.\n32: //\n33: // The kubelet discovers pod updates from 3 sources: file, http, and\n34: // apiserver. Pods from non-apiserver sources are called static pods, and API\n35: // server is not aware of the existence of static pods. In order to monitor\n36: // the status of such pods, the kubelet creates a mirror pod for each static\n37: // pod via the API server.\n38: //\n39: // A mirror pod has the same pod full name (name and namespace) as its static\n40: // counterpart (albeit different metadata such as UID, etc). By leveraging the\n41: // fact that the kubelet reports the pod status using the pod full name, the\n42: // status of the mirror pod always reflects the actual status of the static\n43: // pod. When a static pod gets deleted, the associated orphaned mirror pod\n44: // will also be removed.\n45: type Manager interface {\n46: \t// GetPodByFullName returns the (non-mirror) pod that matches full name, as well as\n47: \t// whether the pod was found.\n48: \tGetPodByFullName(podFullName string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n49: \t// GetPodByName provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches namespace and\n50: \t// name, as well as whether the pod was found.\n51: \tGetPodByName(namespace, name string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n52: \t// GetPodByUID provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches pod UID, as well as\n53: \t// whether the pod is found.\n54: \tGetPodByUID(types.UID) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n55: \t// GetPodByMirrorPod returns the static pod for the given mirror pod and\n56: \t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\n57: \tGetPodByMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n58: \t// GetMirrorPodByPod returns the mirror pod for the given static pod and\n59: \t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\n60: \tGetMirrorPodByPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n61: \t// GetPodAndMirrorPod returns the complement for a pod - if a pod was provided\n62: \t// and a mirror pod can be found, return it. If a mirror pod is provided and\n63: \t// the pod can be found, return it and true for wasMirror.\n64: \tGetPodAndMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (pod, mirrorPod *v1.Pod, wasMirror bool)\n65: \n66: \t// GetPods returns the regular pods bound to the kubelet and their spec.\n67: \tGetPods() []*v1.Pod\n68: \n69: \t// GetPodsAndMirrorPods returns the set of pods, the set of mirror pods, and\n70: \t// the pod fullnames of any orphaned mirror pods.\n71: \tGetPodsAndMirrorPods() (allPods []*v1.Pod, allMirrorPods []*v1.Pod, orphanedMirrorPodFullnames []string)\n72: \n73: \t// GetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap return a map of static pod to its corresponding\n74: \t// mirror pods. It is possible that there is no mirror pod for a static pod\n75: \t// if kubelet is running in standalone mode or is in the process of creating\n76: \t// the mirror pod and in that case, the mirror pod is nil.\n77: \tGetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap() map[*v1.Pod]*v1.Pod\n78: \n79: \t// SetPods replaces the internal pods with the new pods.\n80: \t// It is currently only used for testing.\n81: \tSetPods(pods []*v1.Pod)\n82: \t// AddPod adds the given pod to the manager.\n83: \tAddPod(pod *v1.Pod)\n84: \t// UpdatePod updates the given pod in the manager.\n85: \tUpdatePod(pod *v1.Pod)\n86: \t// RemovePod deletes the given pod from the manager.  For mirror pods,\n87: \t// this means deleting the mappings related to mirror pods.  For non-\n88: \t// mirror pods, this means deleting from indexes for all non-mirror pods.\n89: \tRemovePod(pod *v1.Pod)\n90: \n91: \t// TranslatePodUID returns the actual UID of a pod. If the UID belongs to\n92: \t// a mirror pod, returns the UID of its static pod. Otherwise, returns the\n93: \t// original UID.\n94: \t//\n95: \t// All public-facing functions should perform this translation for UIDs\n96: \t// because user may provide a mirror pod UID, which is not recognized by\n97: \t// internal Kubelet functions.\n98: \tTranslatePodUID(uid types.UID) kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID\n99: \t// GetUIDTranslations returns the mappings of static pod UIDs to mirror pod\n100: \t// UIDs and mirror pod UIDs to static pod UIDs.\n101: \tGetUIDTranslations() (podToMirror map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]kubetypes.MirrorPodUID, mirrorToPod map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID)\n102: }\n103: \n104: // basicManager is a functional Manager.\n105: //\n106: // All fields in basicManager are read-only and are updated calling SetPods,\n107: // AddPod, UpdatePod, or RemovePod.\n108: type basicManager struct {\n109: \t// Protects all internal maps.\n110: \tlock sync.RWMutex\n111: \n112: \t// Regular pods indexed by UID.\n113: \tpodByUID map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]*v1.Pod\n114: \t// Mirror pods indexed by UID.\n115: \tmirrorPodByUID map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]*v1.Pod\n116: \n117: \t// Pods indexed by full name for easy access.\n118: \tpodByFullName       map[string]*v1.Pod\n119: \tmirrorPodByFullName map[string]*v1.Pod\n120: \n121: \t// Mirror pod UID to pod UID map.\n122: \ttranslationByUID map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID\n123: }\n124: \n125: // NewBasicPodManager returns a functional Manager.\n126: func NewBasicPodManager() Manager {\n127: \tpm := &basicManager{}\n128: \tpm.SetPods(nil)\n129: \treturn pm\n130: }\n131: \n132: // SetPods set the internal pods based on the new pods.\n133: func (pm *basicManager) SetPods(newPods []*v1.Pod) {\n134: \tpm.lock.Lock()\n135: \tdefer pm.lock.Unlock()\n136: \n137: \tpm.podByUID = make(map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]*v1.Pod)\n138: \tpm.podByFullName = make(map[string]*v1.Pod)\n139: \tpm.mirrorPodByUID = \tpm.updatePodsInternal(newPods...)\n144: }\n145: \n146: func (pm *basicManager) AddPod(pod *v1.Pod) {\n147: \tpm.UpdatePod(pod)\n148: }\n149: \n150: func (pm *basicManager) UpdatePod(pod *v1.Pod) {\n151: \tpm.lock.Lock()\n152: \tdefer pm.lock.Unlock()\n153: \tpm.updatePodsInternal(pod)\n154: }\n155: \n156: // updateMetrics updates the metrics surfaced by the pod manager.\n157: // oldPod or newPod may be nil to signify creation or deletion.\n158: func updateMetrics(oldPod, newPod *v1.Pod) {\n159: \tvar numEC int\n160: \tif oldPod != nil {\n161: \t\tnumEC -= len(oldPod.Spec.EphemeralContainers)\n162: \t}\n163: \tif newPod != nil {\n164: \t\tnumEC += len(newPod.Spec.EphemeralContainers)\n165: \t}\n166: \tif numEC != 0 {\n167: \t\tmetrics.ManagedEphemeralContainers.Add(float64(numEC))\n168: \t}\n169: }\n170: \n171: // updatePodsInternal replaces the given pods in the current state of the\n172: // manager, updating the various indices. The caller is assumed to hold the\n173: // lock.\n174: func (pm *basicManager) updatePodsInternal(pods ...*v1.Pod) {\n175: \tfor _, pod := range pods {\n176: \t\tpodFullName := kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(pod)\n177: \t\t// This logic relies on a static pod and its mirror to have the same name.\n178: \t\t// It is safe to type convert here due to the IsMirrorPod guard.\n179: \t\tif kubetypes.IsMirrorPod(pod) {\n180: \t\t\tmirrorPodUID := kubetypes.MirrorPodUID(pod.UID)\n181: \t\t\tpm.mirrorPodByUID[mirrorPodUID] = pod\n182: \t\t\tpm.mirrorPodByFullName[podFullName] = pod\n183: \t\t\tif p, ok := pm.podByFullName[podFullName]; ok {\n192: \t\t\t\tpm.translationByUID[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID(mirror.UID)] = resolvedPodUID\n193: \t\t\t}\n194: \t\t}\n195: \t}\n196: }\n197: \n198: func (pm *basicManager) RemovePod(pod *v1.Pod) {\n199: \tupdateMetrics(pod, nil)\n200: \tpm.lock.Lock()\n201: \tdefer pm.lock.Unlock()\n202: \tpodFullName := kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(pod)\n203: \t// It is safe to type convert here due to the IsMirrorPod guard.\n204: \tif kubetypes.IsMirrorPod(pod) {\n205: \t\tmirrorPodUID := kubetypes.MirrorPodUID(pod.UID)\n206: \t\tdelete(pm.mirrorPodByUID, mirrorPodUID)\n207: \t\tdelete(pm.mirrorPodByFullName, podFullName)\n208: \t\tdelete(pm.translationByUID, mirrorPodUID)\n209: \t} else {\n210: \t\tdelete(pm.podByUID, kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID(pod.UID))\n211: \t\tdelete(pm.podByFullName, podFullName)\n212: \t}\n213: }\n214: \n215: func (pm *basicManager) GetPods() []*v1.Pod {\n216: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n217: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n218: \treturn podsMapToPods(pm.podByUID)\n219: }\n220: \n221: func (pm *basicManager) GetPodsAndMirrorPods() (allPods []*v1.Pod, allMirrorPods []*v1.Pod, orphanedMirrorPodFullnames []string) {\n222: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n223: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n224: \tallPods = podsMapToPods(pm.podByUID)\n225: \tallMirrorPods = mirrorPodsMapToMirrorPods(pm.mirrorPodByUID)\n226: \n227: \tfor podFullName := range pm.mirrorPodByFullName {\n228: \t\tif _, ok := pm.podByFullName[podFullName]; mirrorPod are associated with each other.\n306: func IsMirrorPodOf(mirrorPod, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n307: \t// Check name and namespace first.\n308: \tif pod.Name != mirrorPod.Name || pod.Namespace != Pod Lifecycle Manager\\nThe pod lifecycle manager consists of multiple components working together:\\n- **Pod Manager** (pkg/kubelet/pod/pod_manager.go): The `Manager` interface and `basicManager` implementation track and manage all pods on the kubelet, maintaining mappings between static pods and their mirror pods. Created via `NewPluginManager()`, it uses desired/actual state of world pattern similar to the volume manager, with a plugin watcher populating desired state and a reconciler managing plugin registration/deregistration.\\n\\n## Integration Point\\nAll these components are instantiated and orchestrated by the main **Kubelet** struct in pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go, created through `NewKubelet()`.
